###########################
# Soviet Events
###########################

add_namespace = soviets

# Communist government in FROM baltic country and they wish to be annexed
country_event = {
	id = soviets.4
	title = soviets.4.t
	desc = soviets.4.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_soviet_in_riga

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = soviets.4.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }

		effect_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { tag = LIT } }
			 	SOV = {
			 		annex_country = {
					target = LIT
					transfer_troops = yes }
					add_named_threat = { threat = 2 name = soviets.4_threat_LIT }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { tag = FIN } }
			 	SOV = {
			 		annex_country = {
					target = FIN
					transfer_troops = yes }
					add_named_threat = { threat = 5 name = soviets.4_threat_FIN }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { tag = EST } }
			 	SOV = {
			 		annex_country = {
					target = EST
					transfer_troops = yes }
					add_named_threat = { threat = 2 name = soviets.4_threat_EST }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { tag = LAT } }
			 	SOV = {
			 		annex_country = {
					target = LAT
					transfer_troops = yes }
					add_named_threat = { threat = 2 name = soviets.4_threat_LAT }
				}
			}
		}

		hidden_effect = {

			 FROM = {
			 	country_event = { id = baltics.6 hours = 6}
			 }
			 news_event = { id = news.69 days = 1 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = soviets.4.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
	}
}

# Communist government in FROM baltic country and they wish to be part puppet
country_event = {
	id = soviets.5
	title = soviets.5.t
	desc = soviets.5.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_soviet_in_riga

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			FROM = {
				save_event_target_as = baltic
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = soviets.5.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { is_subject = no }
			}
			SOV = { puppet = FROM }
		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { tag = LIT } }
				add_named_threat = { threat = 1 name = soviets.5_threat_LIT }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { tag = FIN } }
				add_named_threat = { threat = 2 name = soviets.5_threat_FIN }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { tag = EST } }
				add_named_threat = { threat = 1 name = soviets.5_threat_EST }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { tag = LAT } }
				add_named_threat = { threat = 1 name = soviets.5_threat_LAT }
			}

		#trigger news event
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event =  { id = news.70 days = 1}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = soviets.5.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
	}
}

#Finland want us to annex them
country_event = {
	id = soviets.12
	title = soviets.12.t
	desc = soviets.12.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_soviet_tank_parade

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Accept
		name = soviets.12.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 75 }
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = FIN
				}
				SOV = {
					add_state_core = PREV
				}
			}
		}
		annex_country = {
			target = FIN
			transfer_troops = yes
		}
		add_threat = 1
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = { days = 1 id = news.69 }
		}
	}

	option = { #Refuse
		name = soviets.12.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 25 }
	}
}

	is_triggered_only = yes

			news_event = { days = 3 id = newsrussia2.1 }
		}
		SOV = {
			puppet = MON
			add_ideas = SOV_Mongolian_advisors
		}
		MON = {
			add_ideas = SOV_Russian_economic_aid
		}
	}
}

# SOV recover territory
country_event = {
	id = soviets.15
	title = soviets.15.t
	desc = soviets.15.d
	picture = GFX_soldiers_with_guns_russia2

	trigger = {
		tag = SOV
		has_idea = SOV_Exiled_russia
		195 = { is_controlled_by = SOV }
		219 = { is_controlled_by = SOV }
		217 = { is_controlled_by = SOV }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 2 }

	option = { # Remove Exiled Russia
		name = soviets.15.a
		remove_ideas = SOV_Exiled_russia
		add_stability = 0.20
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = { days = 2 id = newsrussia2.14 }
		}
	}
}

# SOV becomes Far Eastern Republic
country_event = {
	id = soviets.16

	trigger = {
		tag = SOV
		has_idea = SOV_Exiled_russia
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 2 }

	hidden = yes

	immediate = {
		SOV = {
			set_cosmetic_tag = FER
		}
		set_global_flag = SOV_became_far_eastern_republic
	}
}

# SOV becomes SOV again
country_event = {
	id = soviets.17

	trigger = {
		tag = SOV
		NOT = {
			has_idea = SOV_Exiled_russia
		}
		has_global_flag = SOV_became_far_eastern_republic
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 2 }

	hidden = yes

	immediate = {
		drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
		clr_global_flag = SOV_became_far_eastern_republic
	}
}

# Peasants Revolt
country_event = {
	id = soviets.18
	title = soviets.18.t
	desc = soviets.18.d
	picture = GFX_battkle_kursk_russia2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Oh no
		name = soviets.18.a
		start_civil_war = {
    		ideology = neutrality
    		size = 0.4
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = { days = 2 id = newsrussia2.15 }
			remove_ideas = SOV_Unhappy_peasants1
			remove_ideas = SOV_Unhappy_peasants2
			remove_ideas = SOV_Unhappy_peasants3
			remove_ideas = SOV_Unhappy_peasants4
			remove_ideas = SOV_Unhappy_peasants5
			remove_ideas = SOV_Unhappy_peasants6
			remove_ideas = SOV_Happy_peasants
			random_other_country = {
				limit = {
					original_tag = SOV
					has_war_with = ROOT
				}
				load_focus_tree = {
					tree = soviet2_focus
					keep_completed = no
				}
				unlock_national_focus = SOV_avoid_purge
				unlock_national_focus = SOV_speak_out_against_stalin
				unlock_national_focus = SOV_counter_revolution
				set_country_flag = nopurge_civil_war
			}
		}
	}
}

#White Death
country_event = {
	id = soviets.19
	title = soviets.19.t
	desc = soviets.19.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_dead_soldiers

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		SOV = { has_government = communism }
		TAG = SOV
		FIN = {
			AND = {
				surrender_progress > 0.05
				has_defensive_war_with = SOV
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 1 }

	option = { #White death strike again !
		name = soviets.19.a
		add_ideas = SOV_White_death
	}
}

#Train New Officers
country_event = {
	id = soviets.20
	title = soviets.20.t
	desc = soviets.20.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_british_inspect_troops

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {	#attack is the best defense
		ai_chance = { factor = 25 }
		name = soviets.20.a
		every_army_leader = {
			add_attack = 1
		}
		add_ideas = SOV_New_officers_attack
	}

	option = { #defense
		ai_chance = { factor = 25 }
		name = soviets.20.b
		every_army_leader = {
			add_defense = 1
		}
		add_ideas = SOV_New_officers_defense
	}

	option = { #logistic
		ai_chance = { factor = 25 }
		name = soviets.20.c
		every_army_leader = {
			add_logistics = 1
		}
		add_ideas = SOV_New_officers_logistics
	}

	option = { #planning
		ai_chance = { factor = 25 }
		name = soviets.20.e
		every_army_leader = {
			add_planning = 1
		}
		add_ideas = SOV_New_officers_planning
	}
}

#Katy≈Ñ Massacre (wtf is up with the name?)
country_event = {
	id = soviets.21
	title = soviets.21.t
	desc = soviets.21.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_polish_army

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		SOV = { has_government = communism }
		TAG = SOV
		96 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = SOV }
		784 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = SOV }
		95 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = SOV }
		94 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = SOV }
		93 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = SOV }
		91 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = SOV }
		89 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = SOV }
		has_country_leader = {
			name = "Joseph Stalin"
			ruling_only = yes
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { months = 8 }

	option = { #Do the massacre
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
		}
		name = soviets.21.a
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = SOV_Katyn_massacre
			days = 630
		}
		add_manpower = -22000
		set_country_flag = katyn_massacre
	}

	option = { #We're not monsters
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}
		name = soviets.21.b
	}
}

#Germany Discovers the Massacre
country_event = {
	id = soviets.22
	title = soviets.22.t
	desc = soviets.22.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_dead_soldiers

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		TAG = GER
		GER = {
			has_war_with = SOV
		}
		SOV = {
			has_country_flag = katyn_massacre
		}
		242 = {
			is_controlled_by = GER
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 10 }

	option = { #Mein Gott !
		name = soviets.22.a
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = { days = 1 id = newsrussia2.23 }
		}
		SOV = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = GER
				modifier = denounced_katyn_massacre
			}
		}
		POL = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = SOV
				modifier = katyn_massacre
			}
		}
	}
}

#No purges completed - decide what to do
country_event = {
	id = soviets.23
	title = soviets.23.t
	desc = soviets.23.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_soviet_purge_politicians

	trigger = {
		has_government = communism
		tag = SOV
		has_global_flag = SOV_fourth_international_fired_rework
		NOT = { has_completed_focus = SOV_great_purge }
		NOT = { has_completed_focus = SOV_avoid_purge }
		NOT = { has_completed_focus = SOV_great_purge2 }
		NOT = {
			focus_progress = {
				focus = SOV_great_purge2
				progress > 0.05
			}
		}
		NOT = { has_country_flag = no_purgenoncivilwar }
		NOT = { has_completed_focus = SOV_another_revolution }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 90
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	#Don't invite trotsky
	option = {
		name = soviets.23.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = soviet.23.a_tt
		set_country_flag = SOV_soviet.48_notrotsky_rework
		add_stability = 0.05
	}

	#Invite back Trotsky
	option = {
		name = soviets.23.b
		custom_effect_tooltip = soviets.23.b_tt
		set_country_flag = SOV_soviet.48_notrotsky_rework
		add_war_support = 0.05
	}
}

# Great Purge - Trial of the Anti-Soviet Trotskyist Center
country_event = {
	id = soviets.25
	title = soviets.25.t
	desc = soviets.25.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_soviet_purge_trial

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = SOV
		NOT = { has_completed_focus = SOV_great_purge }
		focus_progress = {
			focus = SOV_great_purge2
			progress > 0.25
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}

	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
		}
		name = soviets.25.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = remove_political_advisor
		show_ideas_tooltip = mikhail_kalinin
		set_country_flag = purged_kalinin
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_ideas = mikhail_kalinin
		}
	}
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
		}
		name = soviets.25.b
		custom_effect_tooltip = remove_political_advisor
		show_ideas_tooltip = nikita_khrushchev
		set_country_flag = purged_khrushchev
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_ideas = nikita_khrushchev
		}
	}
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
		}
		name = soviets.25.c
		custom_effect_tooltip = remove_political_advisor
		show_ideas_tooltip = SOV_ivan_maisky
		set_country_flag = purged_maisky
		set_country_flag = purged_party_members
		custom_effect_tooltip = only_molotov_will_remain
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_ideas = SOV_ivan_maisky
		}
	}
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
		name = soviets.25.e
		set_country_flag = no_political_purge
		custom_effect_tooltip = soviets.27_tt2
	}
}

# Great Purge - Secret Trial of the Generals
country_event = {
	id = soviets.26
	title = soviets.26.t
	desc = soviets.26.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_soviet_purge_officers_01

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = SOV
		NOT = { has_completed_focus = SOV_great_purge }
		focus_progress = {
			focus = SOV_great_purge2
			progress > 0.5
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}

	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}
		name = soviets.26.a
		set_country_flag = purge_1_group_a
		set_country_flag = purge_1_group_alternative_a
		custom_effect_tooltip = remove_theorist
		show_ideas_tooltip = mikhail_tukhachevsky
		custom_effect_tooltip = remove_chief_of_army
		show_ideas_tooltip = alexander_yegorov
		show_ideas_tooltip = vasily_blucher
		custom_effect_tooltip = remove_chief_of_navy
		show_ideas_tooltip = pyotr_smirnov
		show_ideas_tooltip = mikhail_frinovsky
		remove_unit_leader = 401 #mikhail_tukhachevsky, field marshal
		remove_unit_leader = 450 #Leonid Govorov
		remove_unit_leader = 451 #Nikolai Berzarin
		remove_unit_leader = 452 #Alexander Gorbatov
		custom_effect_tooltip = soviets.27_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_ideas = mikhail_tukhachevsky
			remove_ideas = alexander_yegorov
			remove_ideas = vasily_blucher
			remove_ideas = pyotr_smirnov
			remove_ideas = mikhail_frinovsky
		}
	}
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 75
		}
		name = soviets.26.b
		set_country_flag = purge_1_group_b
		set_country_flag = purge_1_group_alternative_b
		custom_effect_tooltip = remove_chief_of_army
		show_ideas_tooltip = semyon_timoshenko
		show_ideas_tooltip = kliment_voroshilov
		custom_effect_tooltip = remove_chief_of_navy
		show_ideas_tooltip = ivan_yumashev
		custom_effect_tooltip = remove_military_high_command
		show_ideas_tooltip = konstantin_rokossovsky
		show_ideas_tooltip = vladimir_kasatonov
		remove_unit_leader = 405 #kliment_voroshilov, field marshal
		remove_unit_leader = 402 #konstantin_rokossovsky, general
		remove_unit_leader = 404 #semyon_timoshenko, general
		remove_unit_leader = 403 #vladimir_kasatonov, naval commander
		custom_effect_tooltip = soviets.27_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_ideas = semyon_timoshenko
			remove_ideas = kliment_voroshilov
			remove_ideas = ivan_yumashev
			remove_ideas = konstantin_rokossovsky
			remove_ideas = vladimir_kasatonov
		}
	}
	# REVISIT Balance, since the latter removes more unit leaders
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
		name = soviets.26.c
		set_country_flag = purge_1_no_purge
		custom_effect_tooltip = soviets.27_tt2
	}
}

# Great Purge - Trial of the 21
country_event = {
	id = soviets.27
	title = soviets.27.t
	desc = soviets.27.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_soviet_purge_officers_02

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = SOV
		NOT = { has_completed_focus = SOV_great_purge2 }
		focus_progress = {
			focus = SOV_great_purge2
			progress > 0.75
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}

	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		name = soviets.27.a
		set_country_flag = purge_2_group_a
		set_country_flag = purge_2_group_alternative_a
		custom_effect_tooltip = remove_political_advisor
		show_ideas_tooltip = SOV_nikolai_yezhov
		custom_effect_tooltip = remove_chief_of_airforce
		show_ideas_tooltip = yakov_smushkevich
		show_ideas_tooltip = pavel_rychagov
		show_ideas_tooltip = alexander_novikov
		custom_effect_tooltip = remove_military_high_command

country_event = {
	id = soviets.42
	title = soviets.42.t
	desc = soviets.42.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_soviet_purge_officers_01

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Bribe his Guards
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		name = soviets.42.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_global_flag = SOV_bribe_guard
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_bribe_guard_tt
		custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_low_kill_chance_tt
		custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_low_risk_chance_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { random_factor_bribe = 0 }
			randomize_temp_variable = {
				var = random_factor_bribe
				distribution = uniform
				min = 0
				max = 100
			}
			round_variable = random_factor_bribe
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = random_factor_bribe
						value = 40
						compare = less_than_or_equals
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = soviets.44 days = 20 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = random_factor_bribe
						value = 50
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = soviets.45 days = 20 }
			}
			else = {
				country_event = { id = soviets.46 days = 10 }
			}
		}
		set_global_flag = SOV_bribe_guard
	}

	option = { #Send an Assassin

			factor = 10
		}

			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = random_factor_assassin
						value = 60
						compare = less_than_or_equals
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = soviets.44 days = 20 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = random_factor_assassin
						value = 70
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = soviets.45 days = 20 }
			}
			else = {
				country_event = { id = soviets.46 days = 10 }
			}
		}
		set_global_flag = SOV_send_assassin
	}

			factor = 80
		}

#Assassination Sucessful
country_event = {
	id = soviets.44
	title = soviets.44.t
	desc = soviets.44.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_soviet_purge_speech

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Perfect
		name = soviets.44.a
		kill_country_leader = yes
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Empty Supreme Soviet of the Soviet Union"
			desc = "POLITICS_EMPTY_PARLIAMENT_DESC"
			picture = "gfx/leaders/SOV/Portrait_Soviet_Empty_Parliament.dds"
			expire = "1965.1.1"
			ideology = stalinism
			traits = {
				empty_parliament
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = { id = newsrussia2.34 days = 1 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					has_global_flag = SOV_bribe_guard
					NOT = { has_global_flag = SOV_try_again }
				}
			}
			add_ideas = SOV_Payment_military
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = SOV_send_assassin
			}
			add_ideas = SOV_Payment_military2
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = SOV_send_squad
			}
		add_ideas = SOV_Payment_military3
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = SOV_armed_bureau
			}
			add_ideas = SOV_Payment_bureaucrats
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = SOV_bomb_bureau
			}
			add_ideas = SOV_Payment_bureaucrats2
		}
		dismantle_faction = yes
	}
}

#The Assassination Attempt Failed
country_event = {

	desc = soviets.45.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Damn
		name = soviets.45.a
		set_global_flag = SOV_civil_war_peace
		set_country_flag = ENG_communist_civil_war
		start_civil_war = {
			ruling_party = communism
    		ideology = communism
    		size = 0.4
			capital = 233
			states = {
				233 232 235 234 231 230 229 232 137 218 238 237 236 217 245
			}
			keep_unit_leaders = {
				401 402 407 410 406 405 403 407 404
			}
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = communism
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = communism
				popularity = 0.88
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = democratic
				popularity = 0.1
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = fascism
				popularity = 0.02
			}
		}

			name = "Empty Supreme Soviet of the Soviet Union"
			desc = "POLITICS_EMPTY_PARLIAMENT_DESC"

				empty_parliament
			}
		}

				limit = {
					original_tag = SOV
					has_government = communism
				}

			}

#Ukrainian Anger
country_event = {
	id = soviets.80
	title = soviets.80.t
	desc = soviets.80.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_riot

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Would You Please Calm Down Thanks
		name = soviets.80.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }

		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_variable = {
			    var = ukrainian_revolt_factor
			    value = 10
			}
			subtract_from_variable = {
			    var = ukrainian_revolt_nothing_happens
			    value = 10
			}

			random_list = {
			    ukrainian_revolt_factor = {
			        country_event = { id = soviets.81 days = 50 }
			    }
			    ukrainian_revolt_nothing_happens = {
			        country_event = { id = soviets.80 days = 50 }
			    }
			    10 = {
			        country_event = { id = soviets.82 days = 50 }
			    }
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
				    var = ukrainian_revolt_factor
				    value = 25
				    compare = less_than_or_equals
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_ukrainian_anger_low_tt
		}

		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
				    var = ukrainian_revolt_factor
				    value = 25
				    compare = greater_than
				}
				check_variable = {
				    var = ukrainian_revolt_factor
				    value = 55
				    compare = less_than
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_ukrainian_anger_medium_tt
		}

		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
				    var = ukrainian_revolt_factor
				    value = 55
				    compare = greater_than_or_equals
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_ukrainian_anger_high_tt
		}

		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			prioritize = { 192 197 196 226 200 227 228 221 259 203 198 199 201 202 193 225 }
			limit = {
				non_damaged_building_level = {
					building = industrial_complex level > 0
				}
			}
			damage_building = {
			    type = industrial_complex damage = 1
			}
		}

		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			prioritize = { 192 197 196 226 200 227 228 221 259 203 198 199 201 202 193 225 }
			limit = {
				non_damaged_building_level = {
					building = arms_factory level > 0
				}
			}
			damage_building = {
			    type = arms_factory damage = 1
			}
		}

		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			prioritize = { 192 197 196 226 200 227 228 221 259 203 198 199 201 202 193 225 }
			limit = {
				non_damaged_building_level = {
					building = infrastructure level > 1
				}
			}
			damage_building = {
			    type = infrastructure
			    damage = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

#Ukrainian Revolt
country_event = {
	id = soviets.81
	title = soviets.81.t
	desc = soviets.81.d
	picture = GFX_cavalry_parade_russia2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Uh Oh...
		name = soviets.81.a

		custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_ukrainian_anger_revolt_tt

		hidden_effect = {
			SOV = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						UKR = {
							exists = no
						}
					}
					release = UKR
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						UKR = {
							is_subject = yes
						}
					}
					set_autonomy = {
					    target = UKR
					    autonomy_state = autonomy_free
					}
				}
			}

			UKR = {
				army_experience = 25
				add_political_power = 150
				leave_faction = yes
				set_popularities = {
					democratic = 0
					neutrality = 0
					fascism = 0
					communism = 100
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = communism
				}
				retire_ideology_leader = communism
				add_ideas = {
					SOV_Ukrainian_revolt
				}
				set_technology = {

#Form the Proletarian Union
country_event = {
	id = soviets.86
	title = soviets.86.t
	desc = soviets.86.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_reichstag_gathering

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = SOV
		SOV = {
			has_government = communism
			num_subjects > 19
			NOT = {
				has_idea = SOV_Exiled_russia
				has_idea = trotskyite_plot
				has_cosmetic_tag = SUW
				has_cosmetic_tag = SOV_proletarian_union
				is_subject = yes
			}
			is_major = yes
			arms_factory > 149
			industrial_complex > 149
			is_faction_leader = yes
			OR = {
				has_completed_focus = SOV_komintern_unite
				has_completed_focus = SOV_workers_world_unite
			}
			OR = {
				OR = {
					16 = {
						is_owned_and_controlled_by = SOV
					}
					any_allied_country = {
						has_government = communism
						has_full_control_of_state = 16
					}
				}
				OR = {
					64 = {
						is_owned_and_controlled_by = SOV
					}
					any_allied_country = {
						has_government = communism
						has_full_control_of_state = 64
					}
				}
				OR = {
					2 = {
						is_owned_and_controlled_by = SOV
					}
					any_allied_country = {
						has_government = communism
						has_full_control_of_state = 2
					}
				}
				OR = {
					126 = {
						is_owned_and_controlled_by = SOV
					}
					any_allied_country = {
						has_government = communism
						has_full_control_of_state = 126
					}
				}
				OR = {
					361 = {
						is_owned_and_controlled_by = SOV
					}
					any_allied_country = {
						has_government = communism
						has_full_control_of_state = 361
					}
				}
				OR = {
					282 = {
						is_owned_and_controlled_by = SOV
					}
					any_allied_country = {
						has_government = communism
						has_full_control_of_state = 282
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Yes!
		name = soviets.86.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				is_subject_of = SOV
			}
			country_event = { id = generics.4 days = 1 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = Trotsky_return
				NOT = {
					has_cosmetic_tag = SUW
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_socialist_meeting_cancel_tt
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = soviets.89 days = 10 }
		}
	}

	option = { #No
		name = soviets.86.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
	}
}

country_event = {

	desc = soviets.103.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		name = soviets.103.a
		add_stability = -0.1
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = democratic
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = democratic
			popularity = 0.20
		}
		dismantle_faction = yes
		remove_ideas = SOV_Army_disorganisation
		hidden_effect = {
			set_rule = {
				can_declare_war_on_same_ideology = no
				can_only_justify_war_on_threat_country = yes
				can_create_factions = yes
			}
			set_division_template_lock = {
				division_template = "Strelkovaya Diviziya"
				is_locked = no
			}
			set_division_template_lock = {
				division_template = "Gornostrelkovaya Diviziya"
				is_locked = no
			}
			set_division_template_lock = {
				division_template = "Motostrelkovaya Diviziya"
				is_locked = no
			}
			set_division_template_lock = {
				division_template = "Kavaleriyskaya Diviziya"
				is_locked = no
			}
			set_division_template_lock = {
				division_template = "NKVD Pogranichnaya Diviziya"
				is_locked = no
			}

				division_template = "Mekhanizirovaniy Korpus"
				is_locked = no
			}
			division_template = {
				name = "Vozdushno-Desantnaya Brigada"

				regiments = {
					paratrooper = { x = 0 y = 0 }

	}

country_event = {
	id = soviets.108
	title = soviets.108.t
	desc = soviets.108.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_read_write

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Accept
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 40
				check_variable = {
					var = russian_investment@ROOT
					value = 1
					compare = equals
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 70
				check_variable = {
					var = russian_investment@ROOT
					value = 2
					compare = equals
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				check_variable = {
					var = russian_investment@ROOT
					value = 3
					compare = equals
				}
			}
		}
		name = soviets.108.a
		FROM = {
			annex_country = {
				target = ROOT
				transfer_troops = yes
			}
		}
		SOV = {
			country_event = { id = soviets.109 }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_game_totally_over_TT
	}

	option = { #Refuse
		trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				var = russian_investment@ROOT
				value = 3
				compare = not_equals
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
			modifier = {
				factor = 60
				check_variable = {
					var = russian_investment@ROOT
					value = 1
					compare = equals
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 30
				check_variable = {
					var = russian_investment@ROOT
					value = 2
					compare = equals
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				check_variable = {
					var = russian_investment@ROOT
					value = 3
					compare = equals
				}
			}
		}
		name = soviets.108.b
		set_country_flag = sov_refused_reunification
		SOV = {
			country_event = { id = soviets.110 }
		}
	}
}

#Second Civil War
country_event = {
	id = soviets.131
	title = soviets.131.t
	desc = soviets.131.d
	picture = GFX_russian_civil_war_russia2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Civil War
		name = soviets.131.a
		hidden_effect = {
			SOU = {
				declare_war_on = {
					target = SOV
					type = second_russian_civil_war
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					has_state_flag = not_white_province
					is_owned_by = SOU
				}
				SOV = {
					add_state_core = PREV
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					has_state_flag = white_province
				}
				SOU = {
					add_state_core = PREV
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					UKR = {
						is_in_faction_with = SOV
					}
				}
				SOU = {
					add_state_core = 201
					add_state_core = 202
					add_state_core = 193
					add_state_core = 225
					add_state_core = 259
					add_state_core = 221
					add_state_core = 228
					add_state_core = 227
					add_state_core = 200
					add_state_core = 226
					add_state_core = 196
					add_state_core = 201
					add_state_core = 197
					add_state_core = 203
					add_state_core = 192
					add_state_core = 198
					add_state_core = 199
				}
				UKR = {
					add_to_war = {
						targeted_alliance = SOV
						enemy = SOU
						hostility_reason = anti_soviet_alliance
					}
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = preparation_done
			SOV = {
				country_event = { id = soviets.187 }
				country_event = { id = soviets.188 }
				country_event = { id = soviets.189 }
			}
			news_event = {
				id = newsrussia2.78 hours = 6
			}
		}
	}
}

#Weapons Cache - Buying Guns Effect

		has_country_flag = buy_weaps
		has_country_flag = second_civil_war_in_progress
		check_variable = {
			var = buy_weapons_count
			value = 0
			compare = greater_than
		}
		#Add a country flag later, like has_country_flag = preparation_over
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 1 }

	option = {
		name = soviets.132.a

			type = infantry_equipment
			amount = buy_weapons_final_count
			producer = SOV
		}
		clr_country_flag = buy_weaps
	}
}

	desc = soviets.133.d

		has_country_flag = second_civil_war_in_progress
		check_variable = {
			var = steal_weapons_count
			value = 0
			compare = greater_than
		}
		#Add a country flag later, like has_country_flag = preparation_over
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 1 }

	option = {
		name = soviets.133.a
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = infantry_equipment
			amount = steal_weapons_final_count
			producer = SOV
		}
		set_temp_variable = { destroy_weapons_final_count = steal_weapons_count }
		multiply_temp_variable = { destroy_weapons_final_count = -1000 }
		SOU = {
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = infantry_equipment
				amount = destroy_weapons_final_count
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = steal_weaps
	}
}

#Sabotage Military Industry
country_event = {
	id = soviets.134

	fire_only_once = yes

	hidden = yes

	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = sabotage_mils
		has_country_flag = second_civil_war_in_progress
		is_in_array = {
			array = sabotage_military_count
			value = 1
		}
		#Add a country flag later, like has_country_flag = preparation_over
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 1 }

	immediate = {
		for_each_loop = {
			array = sabotage_military_count
			value = current #Should always be 1 for now, but can be useful in case we want to go deeper with the decisions
			index = i

			SOU = {
				random_owned_controlled_state = {
					limit = {
						arms_factory > current
					}
					remove_building = {
						type = arms_factory
						level = current
					}
				}
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = sabotage_mils
	}
}

#Ukraine Revolts
country_event = {
	id = soviets.136
	title = soviets.136.t
	desc = soviets.136.d
	picture = GFX_broken_tank_russia2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Ask Them to Join Us - No Country Flag
		name = soviets.136.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 20 }
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = sympathize_with_ukraine
			}
		}
		UKR = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = ukraine_may_join_soviet_side
			country_event = { id = ukrains.1 hours = 6 }
			hidden_effect = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = neutrality
				}
				set_popularities = {
					democratic = 25
					neutrality = 45
					fascism = 15
					communism = 15
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Ask Them to Join Us - Has Country Flag

			has_country_flag = sympathize_with_ukraine
		}
		UKR = {

				}
				set_popularities = {
					democratic = 25
					neutrality = 45

					communism = 15
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Ask Them to stay Neutral During the Conflict

			factor = 80
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				SOV = {
					has_country_flag = sympathize_with_ukraine
				}
			}
		}
		UKR = {

				}

					democratic = 25

					communism = 15
				}
			}
		}	
	}

	option = { #Declare War on Them for Some Random Reason ?!
		name = soviets.136.e

			factor = 0
		}
		declare_war_on = {
			target = UKR
			type = annex_everything
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			SOU = {
				give_military_access = UKR
			}
			UKR = {
				set_popularities = {
					democratic = 25
					neutrality = 45
					fascism = 15
					communism = 15
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_owned_by = UKR
				}
				SOV = {
					add_state_core = PREV
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Russia Asks for Karelia
country_event = {
	id = soviets.141
	title = soviets.141.t
	desc = soviets.141.d
	picture = GFX_cavalry_parade_russia2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Okay
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 25
				OR = {
					is_major = yes
					any_country = {
						is_major = yes
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}
		name = soviets.141.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_war_with = SOV
			}
			white_peace = {
				tag = SOV
				message = SURRENDER_KARELIA_MESSAGE
			}
		}
		SOV = {
			country_event = { id = soviets.142 days = 1 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_country = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
					owns_state = 213
					NOT = {
						tag = ROOT
					}
				}
 			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_karelia_213_subject_tt
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				any_country = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
					owns_state = 215
					NOT = {
						tag = ROOT
					}
				}
 			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_karelia_215_subject_tt
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				any_country = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
					owns_state = 216
					NOT = {
						tag = ROOT
					}
				}
 			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_karelia_216_subject_tt
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				all_owned_state = {
					OR = {
						state = 213
						state = 215
						state = 216
					}
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_game_totally_over_TT
		}
	}

	option = { #No
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 25
				OR = {
					is_major = yes
					any_country = {
						is_major = yes
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}
		name = soviets.141.b
		SOV = {
			country_event = { id = soviets.143 days = 1 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_country = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
					owns_state = 213
					NOT = {
						tag = ROOT
					}
				}
 			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_karelia_213_subject_tt
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				any_country = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
					owns_state = 215
					NOT = {
						tag = ROOT
					}
				}
 			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_karelia_215_subject_tt
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				any_country = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
					owns_state = 216
					NOT = {
						tag = ROOT
					}
				}
 			}

#We give back Karelia
country_event = {
	id = soviets.142
	title = soviets.142.t
	desc = soviets.142.d
	picture = GFX_handshake_russia2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Take back the Land
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		name = soviets.142.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					FROM = {
						owns_state = 213
					}
					any_country = {
						is_subject_of = FROM
						owns_state = 213
					}
				}
			}
			transfer_state = 213
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					FROM = {
						owns_state = 215
					}
					any_country = {
						is_subject_of = FROM
						owns_state = 215
					}
				}
			}
			transfer_state = 215
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					FROM = {
						owns_state = 216
					}
					any_country = {
						is_subject_of = FROM
						owns_state = 216
					}
				}
			}
			transfer_state = 216
		}
	}

	option = { #Keep them as a puppet
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		name = soviets.142.b
		trigger = {
			KAR = {
				exists = yes
				is_subject_of = FROM
				OR = {
					owns_state = 216
					owns_state = 215
					owns_state = 213
				}
			}
		}
		puppet = KAR
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = SOV_freedom_all
				}
				set_autonomy = {
					target = KAR
					autonomy_state = autonomy_russian_protectorate
				}
			}
			else = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = KAR
					autonomy_state = autonomy_supervised_state
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					owns_state = 213
				}
			}
			transfer_state = 213
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					owns_state = 215
				}
			}
			transfer_state = 215
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					owns_state = 216
				}
			}
			transfer_state = 216
		}
	}
}

				type = alliance
				id = SOV
				value = 500
			}
		}
	}

			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = SOV
				is_faction_leader = yes
			}
			add_to_faction = ROOT
			if = {
				limit = {
					any_country = {
						is_in_faction_with = SOV
						is_faction_leader = yes
						NOT = {
							tag = SOV
						}
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = soviets.257 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		SOV = {
			country_event = { id = soviets.155 days = 1 }
		}
		ROOT = {
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = alliance
				id = SOV
				value = 100
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				SOV = {
					is_faction_leader = no
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction_with = SOV
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
				ROOT = {
					add_ai_strategy = {
						type = alliance
						id = PREV
						value = 100
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 60
				OR = {
					is_faction_leader = yes
					any_country = {
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
						is_major = yes
					}
					SOV = {
						has_war = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		name = soviets.154.b
		SOV = {
			country_event = { id = soviets.156 days = 1 }
		}
	}
}

			factor = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 35
				OR = {
					is_major = yes
					any_country = {

						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}
		name = soviets.159.a

#We give back Karelia - Industry
country_event = {
	id = soviets.160
	title = soviets.160.t
	desc = soviets.160.d
	picture = GFX_handshake_russia2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		name = soviets.160.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_idea = SOV_Karelia_payment
				}
			}
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = SOV_Karelia_payment
				days = 180
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					FROM = {
						owns_state = 213
					}
					any_country = {
						is_subject_of = FROM
						owns_state = 213
					}
				}
			}
			transfer_state = 213
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					FROM = {
						owns_state = 215
					}
					any_country = {
						is_subject_of = FROM
						owns_state = 215
					}
				}
			}
			transfer_state = 215
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					FROM = {
						owns_state = 216
					}
					any_country = {
						is_subject_of = FROM
						owns_state = 216
					}
				}
			}
			transfer_state = 216
		}
	}

	option = { #Keep them as a puppet
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		name = soviets.160.b
		trigger = {
			KAR = {
				exists = yes
				is_subject_of = FROM
				OR = {
					owns_state = 216
					owns_state = 215
					owns_state = 213
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_idea = SOV_Karelia_payment
				}
			}
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = SOV_Karelia_payment
				days = 180
			}
		}
		puppet = KAR
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = SOV_freedom_all
				}
				set_autonomy = {
					target = KAR
					autonomy_state = autonomy_russian_protectorate
				}
			}
			else = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = KAR
					autonomy_state = autonomy_supervised_state
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					owns_state = 213
				}
			}
			transfer_state = 213
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					owns_state = 215
				}
			}
			transfer_state = 215
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					owns_state = 216
				}
			}
			transfer_state = 216
		}
	}
}

#Liberate Caucasus if the Player Has the Country Flag
country_event = {
	id = soviets.173

	hidden = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		if= {
			limit = {
				SOV = {
					has_country_flag = control_caucasus
				}
			}
			SOU = {
				release = GEO
				release = AZR
				release = ARM
				add_state_core = 231
				add_state_core = 230
				add_state_core = 229
			}
			SOV = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = GEO
					autonomy_state = autonomy_dominion
				}
			}
			SOV = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = ARM
					autonomy_state = autonomy_dominion
				}
			}
			SOV = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = AZR
					autonomy_state = autonomy_dominion
				}
			}
			GEO = {
				random_owned_state = {
					add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 2
					add_building_construction = {
						type = arms_factory
						level = 2
						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
				division_template = {
					name = "Georgian Imperial Division"
					priority = 1
					regiments = {
						infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
						infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
						infantry = { x = 0 y = 2 }

#Invite Slavic Nation
country_event = {
	id = soviets.178
	title = soviets.178.t
	desc = soviets.178.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_finnish_letter

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Join
		name = soviets.178.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 75
			modifier = {
				factor = 5
				tag = BUL
				any_country = {
					OR = {
						tag = SOV
						tag = MAC
					}
					is_in_faction_with = SOV
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 25
				any_country = {
					is_major = yes
					has_war_with = SOV
				}
			}
		}
		SOV = {
			add_to_faction = ROOT
			country_event = { id = soviets.182 days = 1 }
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FROM
			modifier = russian_diplomats
		}
		ROOT = {
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = alliance
				id = SOV
				value = 500
			}
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = befriend
				id = SOV
				value = 2
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Demand Claims
		name = soviets.178.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 75
				any_country = {
					OR = {
						tag = SOV
						tag = MAC
					}
					is_in_faction_with = SOV
				}
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			tag = BUL
		}
		SOV = {
			country_event = { id = bulgarias.1 days = 1 }
		}
	}

	option = { #Refuse
		name = soviets.178.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 20
				tag = BUL
				any_country = {
					OR = {
						tag = SOV
						tag = MAC
					}
					is_in_faction_with = SOV
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 75
				any_country = {
					is_major = yes
					has_war_with = SOV
				}
			}
		}
		SOV = {
			country_event = { id = soviets.183 days = 1 }
		}
	}
}

	title = soviets.180.t
	desc = soviets.180.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_czech_soldiers_01

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = soviets.180.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
	}
}

#Invite Non Slavic Nation
country_event = {
	id = soviets.181
	title = soviets.181.t
	desc = soviets.181.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_romania_poland_visit

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Join
		name = soviets.181.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 75
			modifier = {
				factor = 25
				any_country = {
					is_major = yes
					has_war_with = SOV
				}
			}
		}
		SOV = {
			add_to_faction = ROOT
			country_event = { id = soviets.182 days = 1 }
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FROM
			modifier = russian_diplomats
		}
		ROOT = {
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = alliance
				id = SOV
				value = 100
			}
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = befriend
				id = SOV
				value = 2
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Refuse
		name = soviets.181.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 75
				any_country = {
					is_major = yes
					has_war_with = SOV
				}
			}
		}
		SOV = {
			country_event = { id = soviets.183 days = 1 }
		}
	}
}

#Opinion Factor for SOU - Civil War

	id = soviets.186

	hidden = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		SOU = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = EST
				modifier = neutral_second_war
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = LAT
				modifier = neutral_second_war
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = FIN
				modifier = neutral_second_war
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = POL
				modifier = neutral_second_war
			}
		}
		EST = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = SOU
				modifier = neutral_second_war
			}
		}
		LAT = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = SOU
				modifier = neutral_second_war
			}
		}
		FIN = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = SOU
				modifier = neutral_second_war
			}
		}

#Event to Add Liberated Countries (Caucasus) Without Creating Too Much World Tension
country_event = {
	id = soviets.187

	hidden = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				SOV = {
					has_country_flag = control_caucasus
				}
			}
			GEO = {
				add_to_war = {
					targeted_alliance = SOV
					enemy = SOU
					hostility_reason = anti_soviet_alliance
				}
			}
			ARM = {
				add_to_war = {
					targeted_alliance = SOV
					enemy = SOU
					hostility_reason = anti_soviet_alliance
				}
			}
			AZR = {
				add_to_war = {
					targeted_alliance = SOV
					enemy = SOU
					hostility_reason = anti_soviet_alliance
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#End of the Civil War - Aftermath
country_event = {
	id = soviets.190
	title = soviets.190.t
	desc = soviets.190.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_ruins

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = soviets.190.a
		set_country_flag = second_civil_war_over
		clr_country_flag = second_civil_war_in_progress
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_subject_of = SOV
			}
			add_ideas = SOV_Isolation
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_subject_of = SOV
			}
			SOV = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = PREV
					autonomy_state = autonomy_free
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = end_civil_war_focus
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = SOU
				}
				remove_core_of = SOU
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = control_central_asia
				}
				KAZ = {
					transfer_state = 406
					transfer_state = 407
					transfer_state = 589
					transfer_state = 588
				}
			}
			582 = {
				remove_province_modifier = {
					static_modifiers = { urals_secret }
					province = 4383
					province = 12200
					province = 7373
					province = 4311
					province = 7300
					province = 10185
					province = 4265
				}
			}
			573 = {
				remove_province_modifier = {
					static_modifiers = { urals_secret }
					province = 12117
					province = 10329
					province = 11223
					province = 7320
					province = 4758
					province = 237
					province = 11307
					province = 278
				}
			}
			581 = {
				remove_province_modifier = {
					static_modifiers = { urals_secret }
					province = 10216
					province = 4874
					province = 12659
					province = 7824
					province = 10551
					province = 10677
					province = 12502
					province = 13076
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_equipment = {
						infantry_equipment > 50000
					}
				}
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = infantry_equipment
					amount = -50000
				}	
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_equipment = {
						infantry_equipment > 40000
					}
					has_equipment = {
						infantry_equipment < 50000
					}
				}
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = infantry_equipment
					amount = -40000
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_equipment = {
						infantry_equipment > 30000
					}
					has_equipment = {
						infantry_equipment < 40000
					}
				}
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = infantry_equipment
					amount = -30000
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_equipment = {
						infantry_equipment > 20000
					}
					has_equipment = {
						infantry_equipment < 30000
					}
				}
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = infantry_equipment
					amount = -20000
				}
			}
			delete_unit_template_and_units = {
				division_template = "Yaponskiy Dobrovol'cheskiy Diviziya"
			}
			delete_unit_template_and_units = {
				division_template = "Ital'yanskiy Dobrovol'cheskiy Diviziya"
			}
		}
		add_threat = -5
		remove_ideas = SOV_Supply_line
		remove_ideas = SOV_Second_civil_war
		remove_ideas = SOV_Urals_secret
		remove_ideas = SOV_Slow_industry
		dismantle_faction = yes
		add_ideas = low_economic_mobilisation
		add_ideas = SOV_Political_Unstability
	}
}

#SOU Annex SOV puppets if it's AI controlled and almost at 100% surrender
country_event = {
	id = soviets.191

	hidden = yes

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		TAG = SOU
		has_war = yes
		SOV = {
			exists = yes
			surrender_progress > 0.75
			has_country_flag = sov_near_capitulation
			is_ai = yes
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 1 }

	immediate = {
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_subject_of = SOV
			}
			SOU = {
				annex_country = {
					target = PREV
					transfer_troops = no
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Contact the German Exiles
country_event = {
	id = soviets.192
	title = soviets.192.t
	desc = soviets.192.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_fascist_gathering

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Yes
		name = soviets.192.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		set_temp_variable = { random_factor_german_exilee = 0 }
		randomize_temp_variable = {
			var = random_factor_german_exilee
			distribution = uniform
			min = 0
			max = 100
		}
		round_variable = random_factor_german_exilee
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = random_factor_german_exilee
						value = 40
						compare = less_than_or_equals
					}
				}
				SOV = {
					country_event = { id = soviets.193 hours = 2 }
				}
			}
			else = {
				SOV = {
					country_event = { id = soviets.194 hours = 2 }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #No
		name = soviets.192.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}
}

#German Exiles Accept
country_event = {
	id = soviets.193
	title = soviets.193.t
	desc = soviets.193.d
	picture = GFX_handshake_russia2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Yay
		name = soviets.193.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		set_country_flag = ger_exiles_accept_puppet
	}
}

#German Exiles Refuse
country_event = {
	id = soviets.194
	title = soviets.194.t
	desc = soviets.194.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_poland_rejects

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Okay, you'll get more freedom
		name = soviets.194.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 75
		}
		set_temp_variable = { random_factor_german_exilee2 = 0 }
		randomize_temp_variable = {
			var = random_factor_german_exilee2
			distribution = uniform
			min = 0
			max = 100
		}
		round_variable = random_factor_german_exilee2
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = random_factor_german_exilee2
						value = 75
						compare = less_than_or_equals
					}
				}
				SOV = {
					country_event = { id = soviets.195 hours = 2 }
				}
			}
			else = {
				SOV = {
					country_event = { id = soviets.196 hours = 2 }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Ask one more time
		name = soviets.194.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
		}
		set_temp_variable = { random_factor_german_exilee = 0 }
		randomize_temp_variable = {
			var = random_factor_german_exilee
			distribution = uniform
			min = 0
			max = 100
		}
		round_variable = random_factor_german_exilee
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = random_factor_german_exilee
						value = 50
						compare = less_than_or_equals
					}
				}
				SOV = {
					country_event = { id = soviets.193 hours = 2 }
				}
			}
			else = {
				SOV = {
					country_event = { id = soviets.196 hours = 2 }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Ok then, bye
		name = soviets.194.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}
}

#Hidden Event to trigger when the player select compensate generals
country_event = {
	id = soviets.207

	hidden = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		set_temp_variable = { random_generals_2 = 0 }
		randomize_temp_variable = {
			var = random_generals_2
			distribution = uniform
			min = 0
			max = 100
		}
		round_variable = random_generals_2
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = random_generals_2
					value = 20
					compare = less_than_or_equals
				}
			}
			SOV = {
				create_corps_commander = {
					name = "Georgy Zhukov"
					picture = "Portrait_Soviet_Gregory_Zhukov.dds"
					traits = { winter_specialist armor_officer media_personality war_hero }
					skill = 5
					attack_skill = 5
					defense_skill = 2
					planning_skill = 4
					logistics_skill = 5
				}
				clr_country_flag = ennemy_second_civil_war_georgy_zhu
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = random_generals_2
					value = 60
					compare = greater_than_or_equals
				}
			}
			SOV = {
				create_corps_commander = {
					name = "Yakov Cherevichenko"
					picture = "Portrait_Soviet_Yakov_Cherevichenko.dds"
					traits = { cavalry_officer }
					skill = 3
					attack_skill = 3
					defense_skill = 3
					planning_skill = 2
					logistics_skill = 2
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			SOV = {
				create_corps_commander = {
					name = "Markian Popov"
					picture = "Portrait_Soviet_Matkian_Popov.dds"
					traits = { winter_specialist infantry_officer brilliant_strategist }
					skill = 2
					attack_skill = 2
					defense_skill = 1
					planning_skill = 2
					logistics_skill = 2
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Hidden Event to trigger when the player select compensate generals - 2
country_event = {
	id = soviets.208

	hidden = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		set_temp_variable = { random_generals_3 = 0 }
		randomize_temp_variable = {
			var = random_generals_3
			distribution = uniform
			min = 0
			max = 100
		}
		round_variable = random_generals_3
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = random_generals_3
					value = 20
					compare = less_than_or_equals
				}
			}
			SOV = {
				create_corps_commander = {
					name = "Ivan Konev"
					picture = "Portrait_Soviet_Ivan_Konev.dds"
					traits = { armor_officer harsh_leader politically_connected }
					skill = 5
					attack_skill = 4
					defense_skill = 5
					planning_skill = 2
					logistics_skill = 5
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = ennemy_second_civil_war_konev
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = random_generals_3
					value = 60
					compare = greater_than_or_equals
				}
			}
			SOV = {
				create_corps_commander = {
					name = "Kirill Meretskov"
					picture = "Portrait_Soviet_Kirill_Meretskov.dds"
					traits = { trait_reckless infantry_officer }
					skill = 3
					attack_skill = 2
					defense_skill = 2
					planning_skill = 3
					logistics_skill = 3
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			SOV = {
				create_corps_commander = {
					name = "Ivan Fedyuninsky"
					picture = "Portrait_Soviet_Ivan_Fedyuninsky.dds"
					traits = { infantry_officer }
					skill = 1
					attack_skill = 1
					defense_skill = 1
					planning_skill = 1
					logistics_skill = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Hidden Event to trigger when the player select compensate generals - 3
country_event = {
	id = soviets.209

	hidden = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		set_temp_variable = { random_generals_4 = 0 }
		randomize_temp_variable = {
			var = random_generals_4
			distribution = uniform
			min = 0
			max = 100
		}
		round_variable = random_generals_4
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = random_generals_4
					value = 20
					compare = less_than_or_equals
				}
			}
			SOV = {
				create_corps_commander = {
					name = "Aleksandr Vasilevsky"
					picture = "Portrait_Soviet_Aleksandr_Vasilevsky.dds"
					traits = { armor_officer politically_connected }
					skill = 4
					attack_skill = 4
					defense_skill = 4
					planning_skill = 3
					logistics_skill = 2
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = ennemy_second_civil_war_vasilevsky
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = random_generals_4
					value = 60
					compare = greater_than_or_equals
				}
			}
			SOV = {
				create_corps_commander = {
					name = "Maksim Purkayev"
					picture = "Portrait_Soviet_Maksim_Purkayev.dds"
					traits = { career_officer }
					skill = 3
					attack_skill = 2
					defense_skill = 3
					planning_skill = 2
					logistics_skill = 3
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			SOV = {
				create_field_marshal = {
					name = "Grigory Kulik"
					picture = "Portrait_Soviet_Grigory_Kulik.dds"
					traits = { old_guard career_officer politically_connected inflexible_strategist }
					skill = 1
					attack_skill = 1
					defense_skill = 1
					planning_skill = 1
					logistics_skill = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Vassalization of Ukraine - Reintegrate the Lost State
country_event = {
	id = soviets.213
	title = soviets.213.t
	desc = soviets.213.d
	picture = GFX_cavalry_parade_russia2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Accepts and Become Puppets
		name = soviets.213.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				SOV = {
					has_country_flag = sympathize_with_ukraine
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = imperial_annexation_lost
		if = {
			limit = {
				SOV = {
					has_country_flag = sympathize_with_ukraine
				}
			}
			SOV = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = UKR
					autonomy_state = autonomy_dominion
				}
				country_event = { id = soviets.214 hours = 6 }
			}
			UKR = {
				set_country_flag = ukraine_no_imperial_govern
			}
		}
		else = {
			SOV = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_idea = SOV_Tsar_we_trust
					}
					set_autonomy = {
						target = UKR
						autonomy_state = autonomy_imperial_governorates
					}
				}
				else = {
					set_autonomy = {
						target = UKR
						autonomy_state = autonomy_puppet
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = soviets.214 hours = 6 }
			}
		}
		remove_ideas = SOV_Isolation
	}

	option = { #Refuse and Stay Independent - Gets National Spirit
		name = soviets.213.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				SOV = {
					has_country_flag = sympathize_with_ukraine
				}
			}
		}
		SOV = {
			country_event = { id = soviets.215 hours = 6 }
		}
		set_country_flag = ukr_refused_vassalization_process
		UKR = {
			add_ideas = SOV_Fight_for_independence
		}
	}
}

				Heir_of_the_Tsar
			}
		}

	}
}

#Option to Cedes South Sakhalin to Japan if In Second Civil War
country_event = {
	id = soviets.227
	title = soviets.227.t
	desc = {
		text = soviets.227.d
		trigger = {
			JAP = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = japan_accept_to_help_give_north_sakhalin
					has_country_flag = japan_accept_to_help_give_russian_far_east
				}	
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = soviets.227.d_2
		trigger = {
			JAP = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = japan_accept_to_help_give_north_sakhalin
					has_country_flag = japan_accept_to_help_give_russian_far_east
				}
			}
		}
	} 
	picture = GFX_report_event_japanese_transport_soldiers

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Ask Non-Agression Pact for North Sakhalin
		trigger = {
			JAP = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = japan_accept_to_help_give_north_sakhalin
					has_country_flag = japan_accept_to_help_give_russian_far_east
				}	
			}
		}
		name = soviets.227.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		JAP = {
			country_event = { id = japans.8 hours = 2 }
		}
	}

	option = { #Never
		trigger = {
			JAP = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = japan_accept_to_help_give_north_sakhalin
					has_country_flag = japan_accept_to_help_give_russian_far_east
				}	
			}
		}
		name = soviets.227.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}

	option = { #Give Them due to the Deal

			JAP = {

					has_country_flag = japan_accept_to_help_give_north_sakhalin

				value = 100
			}

#Germany Has Been Defeated and the Negotiation Was Succesful - Bring Back German Monarchy
country_event = {
	id = soviets.228
	title = soviets.228.t
	desc = soviets.228.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_reichstag_gathering

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		original_tag = SOV
		has_war = no
		is_subject = no
		OR = {
			has_country_flag = ger_exiles_accept_puppet
			has_country_flag = ger_exiles_accept_puppet_reduced
			has_country_flag = ger_exiles_accept_no_puppet
		}
		OR = {
			AND = {
				NOT = {
					country_exists = GER
				}
				OR = {
					SOV = {
						any_owned_state = {
							is_core_of = GER
						}
					}
					any_country = {
						any_owned_state = {
							is_core_of = GER
						}
						is_in_faction_with = SOV
					}
				}
			}
			GER = {
				is_subject_of = SOV
			}
			any_country = {
				GER = {
					is_subject_of = PREV
				}
				is_in_faction_with = SOV
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 10
	}

	option = {
		name = soviets.228.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = ger_exiles_accept_puppet
			}
			ROOT = {
				add_war_support = 0.05
				add_political_power = 50
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							country_exists = GER
						}
					}
					release_autonomy = {
						target = GER
						autonomy_state = autonomy_imperial_governorates
						freedom_level = 0.5
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						country_exists = GER
					}
					set_autonomy = {
						target = GER
						autonomy_state = autonomy_imperial_governorates
					}
				}
			}
			GER = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = neutrality
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					set_popularities = {
						democratic = 25
						neutrality = 50
						fascism = 10
						communism = 15
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						date < 1941.06.04
					}
					create_country_leader = {
						name = "Wilhelm II"
						desc = "POLITICS_WILHELM_II_DESC"
						picture = GFX_portrait_ger_wilhelm_ii
						expire = "1965.1.1"
						ideology = despotism
						traits = {
							anti_democrat imperial_connections
						}
					}
				}
				else = {
					create_country_leader = {
						name = "Wilhelm III"
						desc = "POLITICS_WILHELM_III_DESC"
						picture = GFX_portrait_ger_wilhelm_iii
						expire = "1965.1.1"
						ideology = despotism
						traits = {
							popular_figurehead2
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = ger_exiles_accept_puppet_reduced
			}
			ROOT = {
				add_stability = 0.05
				add_war_support = 0.05
				add_political_power = 100
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							country_exists = GER
						}
					}
					release_autonomy = {
						target = GER
						autonomy_state = autonomy_dominion
						freedom_level = 0.5
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						country_exists = GER
					}
					set_autonomy = {
						target = GER
						autonomy_state = autonomy_dominion
					}
					GER = {
						set_cosmetic_tag = GEC
					}
				}
			}
			GER = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = neutrality
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					set_popularities = {
						democratic = 25
						neutrality = 50
						fascism = 10
						communism = 15
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						date < 1941.06.04
					}
					create_country_leader = {
						name = "Wilhelm II"
						desc = "POLITICS_WILHELM_II_DESC"
						picture = GFX_portrait_ger_wilhelm_ii
						expire = "1965.1.1"
						ideology = despotism
						traits = {
							anti_democrat imperial_connections
						}
					}
				}
				else = {
					create_country_leader = {
						name = "Wilhelm III"
						desc = "POLITICS_WILHELM_III_DESC"
						picture = GFX_portrait_ger_wilhelm_iii
						expire = "1965.1.1"
						ideology = despotism
						traits = {
							popular_figurehead2
						}
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = GER_dominion_no_imperial
				set_country_flag = germany_no_imperial_transform
			}
		}
		else = {
			ROOT = {
				add_stability = 0.1
				add_war_support = 0.1
				add_political_power = 200
				if = {
					limit = {
						GER = {
							is_subject_of = ROOT
						}
					}
					release_puppet = GER
				}
				else = {
					release = GER
				}	
				add_to_faction = GER
			}
			GER = {
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = alliance
					id = SOV
					value = 200
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = neutrality
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					set_popularities = {
						democratic = 25
						neutrality = 50
						fascism = 10
						communism = 15
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						date < 1941.06.04
					}
					create_country_leader = {
						name = "Wilhelm II"
						desc = "POLITICS_WILHELM_II_DESC"
						picture = GFX_portrait_ger_wilhelm_ii
						expire = "1965.1.1"
						ideology = despotism
						traits = {
							anti_democrat imperial_connections
						}
					}
				}
				else = {
					create_country_leader = {
						name = "Wilhelm III"
						desc = "POLITICS_WILHELM_III_DESC"
						picture = GFX_portrait_ger_wilhelm_iii
						expire = "1965.1.1"
						ideology = despotism
						traits = {
							popular_figurehead2
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					GER = {
						is_subject = yes
					}
				}
				PREV = {
					set_autonomy = {
						target = GER
						autonomy_state = autonomy_free
					}
				}
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = GER
				any_country = {
					OR = {
						is_in_faction_with = SOV #GER or ROOT or whatever
						is_subject_of = SOV
					}
					owns_state = PREV
					NOT = { TAG = GER }
				}
			}
			GER = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				any_state = {
					is_owned_by = PREV
					is_core_of = GER
				}
				NOT = {
					TAG = GER
					is_in_faction_with = SOV
					is_subject_of = SOV
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = soviets.229 days = 1 }
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = AUS
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ITA
				}
				any_country = {
					OR = {
						is_in_faction_with = SOV
						is_subject_of = SOV
						TAG = SOV
					}
					owns_state = PREV
				}
			}
			AUS = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
			SOV = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = AUS
					autonomy_state = autonomy_puppet
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				POL = {
					is_subject_of = SOV
				}
				SOV = {
					has_country_flag = poland_accept_imperial_puppet
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = POL
					any_country = {
						OR = {
							TAG = SOV
							TAG = GER
							is_in_faction_with = SOV
							is_subject_of = SOV
						}
						owns_state = PREV
					}
				}
				POL = {
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = CZE
				any_country = {
					OR = {
						is_in_faction_with = SOV
						is_subject_of = SOV
						TAG = SOV
					}
					owns_state = PREV
				}
			}
			CZE = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
			SOV = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = CZE
					autonomy_state = autonomy_puppet
				}
			}	
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = FRA
				any_country = {
					OR = {
						is_in_faction_with = SOV
						is_subject_of = SOV
						TAG = SOV
					}
					owns_state = PREV
				}
			}
			FRA = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}	
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = {
				id = newsrussia2.97 days = 2
			}	
		}
		set_country_flag = restoration_german_monarchy_kaiser
	}
}

				is_major = yes
			}
		}
		every_owned_state = {

				is_core_of = GER
			}
			GER = {
				transfer_state = PREV

		}

			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 60

			}
		}

				is_core_of = GER

			}
		}

		}
	}

#Cannot Reinstore the German Monarchy - Player Gets Event Telling Him What to do
country_event = {
	id = soviets.232
	title = soviets.232.t
	desc = soviets.232.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_reichstag_gathering

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		TAG = SOV
		has_war = no
		SOV = {
			is_subject = no
		}
		OR = {
			has_country_flag = ger_exiles_accept_puppet
			has_country_flag = ger_exiles_accept_puppet_reduced
			has_country_flag = ger_exiles_accept_no_puppet
		}
		any_country = {
			GER = {
				is_subject_of = PREV
			}
			NOT = {
				is_in_faction_with = SOV
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			GER = {
				is_subject_of = SOV
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 10
	}

	option = { #Send Ultimatum
		name = soviets.232.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					is_in_faction_with = SOV
				}
				GER = {
					is_subject_of = PREV
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = soviets.233 days = 2 }
		}
	}

	option = { #Declare War
		name = soviets.232.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		SOV = {
			declare_war_on = {
				target = GER
				type = puppet_wargoal_focus
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Do Nothing
		name = soviets.232.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = anger_german_monarchist
		clr_country_flag = ger_exiles_accept_puppet
		clr_country_flag = ger_exiles_accept_puppet_reduced
		clr_country_flag = ger_exiles_accept_no_puppet
	}
}

#Event for SOU to Release SOV if it Win the Civil War
country_event = {
	id = soviets.238
	title = soviets.238.t
	desc = soviets.238.d

	trigger = {
		TAG = SOU
		NOT = {
			country_exists = SOV
		}

			has_war = no
			is_subject = no
		}
	}

		days = 10
	}

				is_core_of = UKR
				is_owned_by = UKR

					add_state_core = PREV

#Annex the Caucasus if the Player Choose to Liberate Them
country_event = {
	id = soviets.239

	hidden = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = control_caucasus
			}
		}
		SOV = {
			add_state_core = 229
			add_state_core = 230
			add_state_core = 231
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = SOV
				any_country = {
					owns_state = PREV
					NOT = {
						TAG = SOV
						TAG = TAN
						TAG = JAP
					}
				}
			}
			SOV = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
	}
}

#Poland After War - Puppet and Germany is Subject
country_event = {
	id = soviets.248
	title = soviets.248.t
	desc = soviets.248.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_hol_cabinet_gerbrandy

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		TAG = SOV
		has_country_flag = poland_accept_imperial_puppet
		is_subject = no
		has_war = no
		has_government = neutrality
		OR = {
			has_country_flag = ger_exiles_accept_puppet
			has_country_flag = ger_exiles_accept_puppet_reduced
			has_country_flag = ger_exiles_accept_no_puppet
		}
		GER = {
			OR = {
				is_subject_of = SOV
				AND = {
					is_in_faction_with = SOV
					has_government = neutrality
				}
			}
		}
		POL = {
			is_subject_of = SOV
		}
		country_exists = POL
		has_country_flag = restoration_german_monarchy_kaiser
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 10
	}

	option = { #Ask to Trade Land for the Three Nations
		name = soviets.248.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70
		}
		GER = {
			country_event = { id = soviets.249 days = 1 }
		}
	}

	option = { #We'll Give Eastern Germany for Eastern Poland
		name = soviets.248.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		trigger = {
			GER = {
				is_subject_of = SOV
			}
			5 = {
				is_owned_by = GER
			}
			763 = {
				is_owned_by = GER
			}
			63 = {
				is_owned_by = GER
			}
			68 = {
				is_owned_by = GER
			}
			66 = {
				is_owned_by = GER
			}
			67 = {
				is_owned_by = GER
			}
		}
		SOV = {
			transfer_state = 96
			transfer_state = 784
			transfer_state = 95
			transfer_state = 94
			transfer_state = 93
			transfer_state = 91
			transfer_state = 89
			add_state_core = 96
			add_state_core = 784
			add_state_core = 95
			add_state_core = 94
			add_state_core = 93
			add_state_core = 91
			add_state_core = 89
		}
		POL = {
			transfer_state = 5
			transfer_state = 763
			transfer_state = 67
			transfer_state = 66
			transfer_state = 68
			transfer_state = 63
			add_state_core = 5
			add_state_core = 763
			add_state_core = 67
			add_state_core = 66
			add_state_core = 68
			add_state_core = 63
			if = {
				limit = {
					188 = {
						is_owned_and_controlled_by = GER
					}
				}
				POL = {
					transfer_state = 188
					add_state_core = 188
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = anger_germany_poland_deal
		hidden_effect = {
			GER = {
				add_ideas = SOV_German_independence_movement
			}
			news_event = {
				id = newsrussia2.99 days = 1
			}		
		}
	}

	option = { #Give Back the German Lands
		name = soviets.248.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}
		GER = {
			transfer_state = 86
			transfer_state = 85
			add_state_core = 86
			add_state_core = 85
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_owned_by = POL
				is_core_of = GER
			}
			GER = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Do Nothing
		name = soviets.248.e
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}
}

#Gets event to Get Poland as A Puppet or Integrate Them After Germany Has Been Puppeted by SOV - Poland Cedes the East
country_event = {
	id = soviets.252
	title = soviets.252.t
	desc = soviets.252.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_conference

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		TAG = SOV
		has_country_flag = has_given_eastern_poland
		is_subject = no
		has_war = no
		has_government = neutrality
		OR = {
			has_country_flag = ger_exiles_accept_puppet
			has_country_flag = ger_exiles_accept_puppet_reduced
			has_country_flag = ger_exiles_accept_no_puppet
		}
		GER = {
			OR = {
				is_subject_of = SOV
				AND = {
					is_in_faction_with = SOV
					has_government = neutrality
				}
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			POL = {
				is_subject_of = SOV
			}
		}
		country_exists = POL
		has_country_flag = restoration_german_monarchy_kaiser
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 10
	}

	option = { #Ask Poland to Become a Puppet
		name = soviets.252.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		POL = {
			country_event = { id = polands.11 days = 1 }
		}
	}

	option = { #Ask Poland to Integrate With Us
		name = soviets.252.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		POL = {
			country_event = { id = polands.14 days = 1 }
		}
	}

	option = { #Let's Leave Them Alone
		name = soviets.252.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}
}

#France Asks for Leadership
country_event = {
	id = soviets.254
	title = soviets.254.t
	desc = soviets.254.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_worried_french

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Okay
		ai_chance = { factor = 80 }
		name = soviets.254.a
		FRA = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					FRA = {
						is_faction_leader = yes
					}
				}
				set_faction_name = entente_reformed
			}
			else = {
				create_faction = entente_reformed
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					SOV = {
						is_faction_leader = yes
					}
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						is_in_faction_with = SOV
					}
					FRA = {
						add_to_faction = PREV
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_to_faction = SOV
			}
		}
		FRA = {
			country_event = { id = soviets.255 days = 1 }
		}
		FRA = {
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = alliance
				id = SOV
				value = 500
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		ai_chance = { factor = 20 }
		name = soviets.254.b
		FRA = {
			country_event = { id = soviets.256 days = 1 }
		}
	}
}

#Gets Event Germany want to regain it's old territories if SOV Owns Them
country_event = {
	id = soviets.259
	title = soviets.259.t
	desc = soviets.259.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_parliament

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		TAG = SOV
		is_subject = no
		has_war = no
		has_government = neutrality
		OR = {
			has_country_flag = ger_exiles_accept_puppet
			has_country_flag = ger_exiles_accept_puppet_reduced
			has_country_flag = ger_exiles_accept_no_puppet
		}		
		GER = {
			OR = {
				is_subject_of = SOV
				AND = {
					is_in_faction_with = SOV
					has_government = neutrality
				}
			}		
		}
		85 = {
			is_owned_and_controlled_by = SOV
		}
		86 = {
			is_owned_and_controlled_by = SOV
		}
	}

	option = { #Return German Lands
		name = soviets.259.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		GER = {
			transfer_state = 86
			transfer_state = 85
			add_state_core = 85
			add_state_core = 86
		}
	}

	option = { #Don't Return German Lands
		name = soviets.259.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				GER = {
					is_subject_of = SOV
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = anger_germany_poland_deal
			hidden_effect = {
				GER = {
					add_ideas = SOV_German_independence_movement
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			GER = {
				leave_faction = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

#End of the Civil War - Aftermath If For Some Reasons the Event Wasn't Triggered After the Capitulation
country_event = {
	id = soviets.260
	title = soviets.260.t
	desc = soviets.260.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_ruins

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = soviets.260.a
		set_country_flag = second_civil_war_over
		clr_country_flag = second_civil_war_in_progress
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_subject_of = SOV
			}
			add_ideas = SOV_Isolation
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_subject_of = SOV
			}
			SOV = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = PREV
					autonomy_state = autonomy_free
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = end_civil_war_focus
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = SOU
				}
				remove_core_of = SOU
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = control_central_asia
				}
				KAZ = {
					transfer_state = 406
					transfer_state = 407
					transfer_state = 589
					transfer_state = 588
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = control_central_asia
				}
				KAZ = {
					transfer_state = 590
					transfer_state = 583
					transfer_state = 402
					transfer_state = 587
				}
				remove_state_core = 590
				remove_state_core = 583
				remove_state_core = 402
				remove_state_core = 587
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = control_caucasus
				}
				delete_unit_template_and_units = {
					division_template = "Kavkazskaya kazach'ya diviziya"
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = train_caucasian_soldiers_civil_war
					has_country_flag = control_caucasus
				}
				delete_unit_template_and_units = {
					division_template = "Opytnyy Kavkazskaya kazach'ya diviziya"
				}
				delete_unit_template_and_units = {
					division_template = "Kavkazskaya kazach'ya diviziya"
				}
			}
			582 = {
				remove_province_modifier = {
					static_modifiers = { urals_secret }
					province = 4383
					province = 12200
					province = 7373
					province = 4311
					province = 7300
					province = 10185
					province = 4265
				}
			}
			573 = {
				remove_province_modifier = {
					static_modifiers = { urals_secret }
					province = 12117
					province = 10329
					province = 11223
					province = 7320
					province = 4758
					province = 237
					province = 11307
					province = 278
				}
			}
			581 = {
				remove_province_modifier = {
					static_modifiers = { urals_secret }
					province = 10216
					province = 4874
					province = 12659
					province = 7824
					province = 10551
					province = 10677
					province = 12502
					province = 13076
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_equipment = {
						infantry_equipment > 40000
					}
				}
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = infantry_equipment
					amount = -40000
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_equipment = {
						infantry_equipment > 30000
					}
					has_equipment = {
						infantry_equipment < 40000
					}
				}
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = infantry_equipment
					amount = -30000
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_equipment = {
						infantry_equipment > 20000
					}
					has_equipment = {
						infantry_equipment < 30000
					}
				}
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = infantry_equipment
					amount = -20000
				}
			}
			delete_unit_template_and_units = {
				division_template = "Yaponskiy dobrovol'cheskiy diviziya"
			}
			delete_unit_template_and_units = {
				division_template = "Ital'yanskiy Dobrovol'cheskiy Diviziya"
			}
		}
		add_threat = -5
		remove_ideas = SOV_Supply_line
		remove_ideas = SOV_Second_civil_war
		remove_ideas = SOV_Urals_secret
		remove_ideas = SOV_Slow_industry
		dismantle_faction = yes
		add_ideas = low_economic_mobilisation
		add_ideas = SOV_Political_Unstability
	}
}

				limit = {

			}

	}

			has_idea = SOV_Political_Unstability
			has_idea = SOV_Political_Unstability2
		}
		surrender_progress > 0.15
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

		days = 10
	}

	option = { #Thank you
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		name = soviets.266.a
		add_political_power = -100
		add_war_support = 0.1

			limit = {
				has_idea = SOV_Political_Unstability
			}
			remove_ideas = SOV_Political_Unstability
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = SOV_Political_Unstability2
			}
			remove_ideas = SOV_Political_Unstability2
		}
	}
}
