#Hidden Event to Kick Retarded (Communist Portugal) Countries Who Shouldn't be in faction with the Russian during the Second Civil War
country_event = {
	id = soviets.268

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			TAG = SOV
			TAG = UKR
			TAG = BLR
			TAG = KAZ
			TAG = TMS
			TAG = GEO
			TAG = ARM
			TAG = AZR
			is_subject = yes
		}
		SOV = {
			has_country_flag = second_civil_war_in_progress
			has_war = yes
		}
		any_country = {
			is_in_faction_with = SOV
			NOT = {
				TAG = UKR
				TAG = BLR
				TAG = KAZ
				TAG = TMS
				TAG = GEO
				TAG = ARM
				TAG = AZR
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 10
	}

	hidden = yes

	immediate = {
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = SOV
				NOT = {
					TAG = UKR
					TAG = BLR
					TAG = KAZ
					TAG = TMS
					TAG = GEO
					TAG = ARM
					TAG = AZR
					TAG = SOV
				}
			}
			leave_faction = yes
			white_peace = SOU
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_war_with = UKR
				}
				white_peace = UKR
			}
		}	
	}
}

#Remove the modifiers if the idea is not valid anymore
country_event = {
	id = soviets.281

	hidden = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = SOV
		NOT = {
			is_subject = no
			has_government = fascism
			has_idea = SOV_Women_fascist_movement
			has_idea = SOV_Otdel_bezopasnosti
		}
		OR = {
			has_dynamic_modifier = {
				modifier = fascist_women_modifiers
			}
			has_dynamic_modifier = {
				modifier = fascist_security_modifiers
			}
		}
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dynamic_modifier = {
					modifier = fascist_women_modifiers
				}
			}
			remove_dynamic_modifier = {
				modifier = fascist_women_modifiers
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dynamic_modifier = {
					modifier = fascist_security_modifiers
				}
			}
			remove_dynamic_modifier = {
				modifier = fascist_security_modifiers
			}
		}
	}
}

#The Fate of Anastasy
country_event = {
	id = soviets.282
	title = soviets.282.t
	desc = soviets.282.d
	picture = GFX_russia2event_anastasy_vonsiatsky

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Accept his return
		name = soviets.282.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = SOV_ai_behavior
					option = ANASTASY_FASCIST
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = SOV_ai_behavior
					option = KONSTANTIN_FASCIST
				}
			}
		}
		add_stability = 0.05
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = soviets.283 days = 100 }
		}
	}

	option = { #Keep small contacts with him
		name = soviets.282.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = SOV_ai_behavior
					option = ANASTASY_FASCIST
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = SOV_ai_behavior
					option = KONSTANTIN_FASCIST
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = soviets.290 days = 100 }
		}
	}

	option = { #Refuse his return
		name = soviets.282.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = SOV_ai_behavior
					option = ANASTASY_FASCIST
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = SOV_ai_behavior
					option = KONSTANTIN_FASCIST
				}
				NOT = {
					controls_state = 366
				}
			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.05
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = soviets.298 days = 100 }
		}
	}

	option = { #Demand the controller of 366 (Florida) to arrest him
		name = soviets.282.e
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				controls_state = 366
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = SOV_ai_behavior
					option = ANASTASY_FASCIST
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = SOV_ai_behavior
					option = KONSTANTIN_FASCIST
				}
			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.1
		hidden_effect = {
			366 = {
				CONTROLLER = {
					country_event = { id = soviets.305 days = 50 }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Arrest him
		name = soviets.282.f
		trigger = {
			controls_state = 366
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = SOV_ai_behavior
					option = ANASTASY_FASCIST
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = SOV_ai_behavior
					option = KONSTANTIN_FASCIST
				}
				controls_state = 366
			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.1
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = soviets.309 days = 50 }
		}
		#This is just in case you control 366, very unlikely
	}
}

					value = 1

			}

	id = soviets.307
	title = soviets.307.t
	desc = soviets.307.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_germany_politician_handshake

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = soviets.307.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FROM
			modifier = refused_arrest
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = soviets.308 days = 100 }
		}
	}
}

#Neutralize Foreign Nuisance Event
country_event = {
	id = soviets.310
	title = soviets.310.t
	desc = soviets.310.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_conference

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Sure
		name = soviets.310.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 75
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				has_government = fascism
			}
		}
		add_stability = 0.05
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = SOV_Root_russian_pact
			days = 730
		}
		set_country_flag = accepted_russian_root_agreement
		diplomatic_relation = {
			country = SOV
			relation = non_aggression_pact
			active = yes
		}
		SOV = {
			country_event = { id = soviets.311 days = 1 }
		}
	}

	option = { #Refuse
		name = soviets.310.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_government = fascism
			}
		}
		add_political_power = 50
		SOV = {
			country_event = { id = soviets.312 days = 1 }
		}
	}
}

#Broken ROOT-Russian Agreement
country_event = {
	id = soviets.313
	title = soviets.313.t
	desc = soviets.313.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_lend_lease

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_ideas = SOV_Root_russian_pact
		}
	}

	option = { #Oh
		name = soviets.313.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_offensive_war_with = SOV
			}
			set_temp_variable = { stability_loss_fascism_factor = ROOT.party_popularity@fascism }
			multiply_temp_variable = { stability_loss_fascism_factor = -1 }
			clamp_temp_variable = {
				var = stability_loss_fascism_factor
				min = -0.25
				max = -0.1
			}
			add_stability = stability_loss_fascism_factor
		}
		else = { #Won't punish the player too hard if SOV is the attacker
			add_stability = -0.05
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			SOV = {
				country_event = soviets.314
			}
			clr_country_flag = accepted_russian_root_agreement
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = is_target_of_russia_with_agreement
				}
				ROOT = {
					add_ai_strategy = {
						type = support
						id = PREV
						value = 1000
					}

					add_ai_strategy = {
						type = alliance
						id = PREV
						value = 1000
					}

					add_ai_strategy = {
						type = send_volunteers_desire
						id = PREV
						value = 1000
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Our Future Foes
country_event = {
	id = soviets.316
	title = soviets.316.t
	desc = soviets.316.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_finnish_letter

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Europe
		name = soviets.316.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_future_foes_tt1
		custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_future_foes_europe_tt
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					original_tag = SOV
				}
				capital_scope = {
					is_on_continent = europe
				}
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = SOV
				modifier = russian_european_focus
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = SOV_fascist_focus_on_europe
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = { id = newsrussia2.117 days = 1 }
		}
	}

	option = { #Asia
		name = soviets.316.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_future_foes_tt2
		custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_future_foes_asia_tt
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					original_tag = SOV
				}
				capital_scope = {
					is_on_continent = asia
				}
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = SOV
				modifier = russian_asian_focus
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = SOV_fascist_focus_on_asia
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = { id = newsrussia2.118 days = 1 }
		}
	}

	option = { #America
		name = soviets.316.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_future_foes_tt3
		custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_future_foes_america_tt
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					original_tag = SOV
				}
				capital_scope = {
					OR = {
						is_on_continent = north_america
						is_on_continent = south_america
					}
				}
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = SOV
				modifier = russian_american_focus
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = SOV_fascist_focus_on_america
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = { id = newsrussia2.119 days = 1 }
		}
	}

	option = { #Defense
		name = soviets.316.e
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
		}
		add_political_power = 100
		custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_future_foes_tt4
		custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_future_foes_closed_tt
		set_country_flag = SOV_fascist_focus_on_defense
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = { id = newsrussia2.120 days = 1 }
		}
	}
}

#Undo the hostile behaviors towards Russian enemies
country_event = {
	id = soviets.317
	
	hidden = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		clr_country_flag = accepted_russian_root_agreement
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = is_target_of_russia_with_agreement
			}
			ROOT = {
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = support
					id = PREV
					value = 1000
				}

				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = alliance
					id = PREV
					value = 1000
				}

				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = send_volunteers_desire
					id = PREV
					value = 1000
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Used for AI strategy, should work fine now, using event instead of on_action to avoid bugs and performance issues
country_event = {
	id = soviets.318
	
	hidden = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			SOV = {
				AND = {
					has_war = yes
					has_country_flag = {
						flag = SOV_ai_strategy_count_enemy_planes
						days > 7
					}
				}
			}
			has_global_flag = {
				flag = SOV_ai_strategy_count_enemy_planes_global
				days > 15
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		clr_country_flag = SOV_ai_strategy_count_enemy_planes
		set_country_flag = SOV_ai_strategy_count_enemy_planes
		clr_global_flag = SOV_ai_strategy_count_enemy_planes_global
		set_global_flag = SOV_ai_strategy_count_enemy_planes_global
		set_variable = { plane_count_enemy_sov = 0 }
		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = SOV.enemies
			break = end_array
			
			set_temp_variable = { temp_var_plane_count = num_deployed_planes }
			SOV = {
				add_to_variable = { plane_count_enemy_sov = temp_var_plane_count }
			}
		}
	}
}

#The fate of FROM
country_event = {
	id = soviets.319
	title = soviets.319.t
	desc = soviets.319.d
	picture = GFX_military_parade_russia2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Demande puppet
		name = soviets.319.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
		}
		event_target:SOV_target_country_fascist = {
			country_event = { id = soviets.320 days = 1 }
		}
		#clear_global_event_target = SOV_target_country_fascist
		#Resets anyways, and causes errors for the next events for some reasons
	}

	option = { #Demande annex
		name = soviets.319.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
		}
		event_target:SOV_target_country_fascist = {
			country_event = { id = soviets.323 days = 1 }
		}
		#clear_global_event_target = SOV_target_country_fascist
	}

	option = { #Enforce military access
		name = soviets.319.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
		}
		event_target:SOV_target_country_fascist = {
			country_event = { id = soviets.326 days = 1 }
		}
		#clear_global_event_target = SOV_target_country_fascist
	}
}

#SOV Demands Puppet
country_event = {
	id = soviets.320
	title = soviets.320.t
	desc = soviets.320.d
	picture = GFX_artillery_with_building_russia2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Ok
		name = soviets.320.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				is_major = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 25
				is_major = no
				OR = {
					any_country = {
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
						is_major = yes
					}
					any_country = {
						has_guaranteed = ROOT
						is_major = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				SOV = {
					has_idea = SOV_Impose_order
				}
			}
			SOV = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = ROOT
					autonomy_state = autonomy_state_magistrate
				}
				country_event = { id = soviets.321 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		else = {
			SOV = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = ROOT
					autonomy_state = autonomy_puppet
				}
				country_event = { id = soviets.321 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = { id = newsrussia2.141 days = 2 }
		}
	}

	option = { #No
		name = soviets.320.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 90
				is_major = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 75
				is_major = no
				OR = {
					any_country = {
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
						is_major = yes
					}
					any_country = {
						has_guaranteed = ROOT
						is_major = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		SOV = {
			country_event = { id = soviets.322 days = 1 }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = { id = newsrussia2.144 days = 2 }
		}
	}
}

#SOV Demands Annex
country_event = {
	id = soviets.323
	title = soviets.323.t
	desc = soviets.323.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_polish_border

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Ok
		name = soviets.323.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_major = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				is_major = no
				OR = {
					any_country = {
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
						is_major = yes
					}
					any_country = {
						has_guaranteed = ROOT
						is_major = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_game_totally_over_TT
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = { id = newsrussia2.140 }
		}
		SOV = {
			annex_country = {
				target = ROOT
				transfer_troops = no
			}
			country_event = { id = soviets.324 days = 1 }
		}
	}

	option = { #No
		name = soviets.323.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				is_major = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 90
				is_major = no
				OR = {
					any_country = {
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
						is_major = yes
					}
					any_country = {
						has_guaranteed = ROOT
						is_major = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = { id = newsrussia2.143 }
		}
		SOV = {
			country_event = { id = soviets.325 days = 1 }
		}
	}
}

#Lost State Receive Events to be Integreated Back to Russia
country_event = {
	id = soviets.335
	title = soviets.335.t
	desc = soviets.335.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_south_africa_patrol

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Yay
		name = soviets.335.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		SOV = {
			annex_country = {
				target = ROOT
			}
			country_event = { id = soviets.336 hours = 12 }
		}
	}

	option = { #No
		name = soviets.335.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
		}
		SOV = {
			country_event = { id = soviets.337 hours = 12 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				SOV = {
					is_ai = no
				}
			}
			ROOT = {
				add_ideas = SOV_Fighting_against_the_russians
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = UKR
				UKR = {
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
			}
			UKR = {
				add_to_faction = ROOT
			}
		}
	}
}

#Russo-German Treaty

	title = soviets.339.t
	desc = soviets.339.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_hol_cabinet_de_geer

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Yes
		name = soviets.339.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 75
		}
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = SOV_Russo_german_treaty_fascist
			days = 180
		}
		diplomatic_relation = {
			country = SOV
			relation = non_aggression_pact
			active = yes
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = SOV
			modifier = accepted_russo_german_treaty
		}
		SOV = {
			country_event = { id = soviets.340 days = 1 }
		}
	}

	option = { #No
		name = soviets.339.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = SOV
			modifier = refused_russo_german_treaty
		}
		SOV = {
			country_event = { id = soviets.341 days = 1 }
		}
	}
}

		}
	}

		}
		name = soviets.345.a

			factor = 25
		}
		add_manpower = -2
		add_war_support = 0.05
		add_political_power = -150
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = GER
			modifier = anti_german_sentiment
		}
		add_ideas = SOV_anti_german_sentiment
		hidden_effect = {
			GER = {
				country_event = { id = soviets.347 days = 1 }
			}
		}
	}

			country_exists = JAP
		}
		name = soviets.345.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
		}
		add_manpower = -2
		add_war_support = 0.05
		add_political_power = -100
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = JAP
			modifier = anti_japanese_sentiment
		}
		add_ideas = SOV_anti_japanese_sentiment
		hidden_effect = {
			JAP = {
				country_event = { id = soviets.347 days = 1 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Blame it on the real murderers

			factor = 25
		}
		add_stability = 0.05
		add_war_support = -0.1

	}

		}

	}
}

		}

					has_id = 515
					has_id = 511
					has_id = 516
					has_id = 517
					has_id = 518
				}
			}
			retire = yes
		}
		set_country_flag = denikin_resigned_fascist
	}
}

#Review our position
country_event = {
	id = soviets.351
	title = soviets.351.t
	desc = soviets.351.d
	picture = GFX_military_parade_kremlin_russia2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Europe
		name = soviets.351.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = SOV_fascist_focus_on_europe
			}
			add_stability = -0.15
			add_war_support = -0.15
		}
		else = {
			add_stability = -0.05
			add_war_support = -0.05
		}
		remove_ideas = SOV_Uncertain_fate
		add_ideas = SOV_Alliance_with_europe
		create_faction = russian_accords
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = { id = newsrussia2.121 days = 1 }
		}
	}

	option = { #Asia
		name = soviets.351.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = SOV_fascist_focus_on_asia
			}
			add_stability = -0.1
			add_war_support = -0.1
		}
		remove_ideas = SOV_Uncertain_fate
		add_ideas = SOV_Alliance_with_asia
		create_faction = russian_accords
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = { id = newsrussia2.122 days = 1 }
		}
	}

	option = { #Closed
		name = soviets.351.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = SOV_fascist_focus_on_defense
			}
			add_stability = 0.1
			add_war_support = 0.1
		}
		else = {
			add_stability = 0.05
			add_war_support = 0.05
		}
		remove_ideas = SOV_Uncertain_fate
		add_ideas = SOV_Closed_alliance
		create_faction = russian_accords
		custom_effect_tooltip = assure_neighbouring_safety_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = { id = newsrussia2.124 days = 1 }
		}
	}
}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		add_state_core = 463
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					owns_state = 463
				}
			}
			transfer_state = 463
		}
	}
}

#Profit from FROM (Russian States)
country_event = {
	id = soviets.360
	title = soviets.360.t
	desc = soviets.360.d
	picture = GFX_military_parade_kremlin_russia2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Great!
		name = soviets.360.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		set_variable = { economicgainfactor = 0 }
		randomize_variable = {
			var = economicgainfactor
			distribution = uniform
			min = 0.5
			max = 3.5
		}
		round_variable = economicgainfactor
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = economicgainfactor
					value = 1
					compare = equals
				}
			}
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
				add_building_construction = {
					type = industrial_complex
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = economicgainfactor
					value = 2
					compare = equals
				}
			}
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
				add_building_construction = {
					type = arms_factory
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = economicgainfactor
					value = 3
					compare = equals
				}
			}
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				limit = {
					is_coastal = yes
				}
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
				add_building_construction = {
					type = dockyard
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Send Profit to SOV
country_event = {
	id = soviets.361

	is_triggered_only = yes

	hidden = yes

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_subject_of = SOV
			}
			set_temp_variable = { nexteconomicevent = 0 }
			randomize_temp_variable = {
				var = nexteconomicevent
				distribution = uniform
				min = 100
				max = 365
			}
			round_temp_variable = nexteconomicevent
			SOV = {
				country_event = { id = soviets.360 days = nexteconomicevent }
			}
		}
	}
}

#Communist Ultimatum
country_event = {
	id = soviets.367
	title = soviets.367.t
	desc = soviets.367.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_soviet_in_riga

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = communist_ultimatum_triggered
			remove_ideas = SOV_Communist_influence_international_3
			clr_country_flag = SOV_AI_is_target_international
			SOV = {
				clr_country_flag = SOV_AI_is_influencing_international
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Civil war
		name = soviets.367.a
		trigger = {
			num_of_controlled_states > 1
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 75
				is_major = yes
			}
		}
		start_civil_war = {
			ruling_party = ROOT
			ideology = communism
			size = party_popularity@communism
		}
		set_country_flag = is_civil_war_international
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = { id = newsrussia2.145 hours = 5 }
			SOV = {
				country_event = { id = soviets.370 }
			}
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					has_civil_war = yes
					has_government = communism
					original_tag = ROOT
					any_country = {
						has_war_with = PREV
						has_civil_war = yes
						has_country_flag = communist_ultimatum_triggered
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = is_communist_triggered_revolution
				add_ideas = SOV_Supporters_fourth_international
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Submit
		name = soviets.367.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 25
				is_major = yes
			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.1
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = communism
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = communism
			popularity = 0.1
		}
		add_ideas = SOV_Supporters_fourth_international
		set_country_flag = submit_communism_international
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = { id = newsrussia2.149 hours = 5 }
			SOV = {
				country_event = { id = soviets.371 }
			}
		}
	}
}

#Civil War!
country_event = {
	id = soviets.383
	title = soviets.383.t
	desc = soviets.383.d
	picture = GFX_soldiers_with_guns_russia2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #UHH
		name = soviets.383.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_subject = yes
				}
				OVERLORD = {
					country_event = soviets.388
					set_autonomy = {
						target = ROOT
						autonomy_state = autonomy_free
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction = yes
				}
				leave_faction = yes
			}
		}
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = SOV_Cold_civil_war
			days = 180
		}
		start_civil_war = {
			ruling_party = ROOT
			ideology = communism
			size = party_popularity@communism
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = { id = newsrussia2.147 hours = 5 }
			SOV = {
				country_event = { id = soviets.384 }
			}
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					has_civil_war = yes
					has_government = communism
					original_tag = ROOT
					any_country = {
						has_war_with = PREV
						has_civil_war = yes
						has_country_flag = civil_war_iron_curtain
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = is_communist_civil_war_iron_curtain
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = SOV_Cold_civil_war
					days = 180
				}
				SOV = {
					add_ai_strategy = {
						type = send_volunteers_desire
						id = PREV
						value = 100
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Give Guided by Russia 2 to all the Puppets
country_event = {
	id = soviets.395

	is_triggered_only = yes

	hidden = yes

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = SOV_Guided_by_russia
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = SOV_Guided_by_russia
				add_idea = SOV_Guided_by_russia2
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_ideas = SOV_Guided_by_russia2
		}
	}
}

#Hidden Event to spawn the Divisions and ships for the Black Revolution
country_event = {
	id = soviets.404

	is_triggered_only = yes

	hidden = yes

	immediate = {
		SOV = {
			load_oob = "SOV_black_revolution_oob"
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = anarchist_hold_leningrad
				}
				load_oob = "SOV_leningrad_ships"
				load_oob = "SOV_naval_ships_black_revolution"
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = anarchist_hold_leningrad
					}
				}
				load_oob = "SOV_naval_ships_black_revolution"
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = anarchist_hold_leningrad
					NOT = {
						has_dlc = "Man the Guns"
					}	
				}
				load_oob = "SOV_leningrad_ships_nomtg"
				load_oob = "SOV_naval_ships_black_revolution_nomtg"
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = anarchist_hold_leningrad
						has_dlc = "Man the Guns"
					}	
				}
				load_oob = "SOV_naval_ships_black_revolution_nomtg"
			}
		}
		SOU = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					SOV = {
						NOT = {
							has_country_flag = anarchist_soldiers_desert
						}
					}
				}
				load_oob = "SOU_black_revolution"
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					SOV = {
						has_country_flag = anarchist_soldiers_desert
					}
				}
				load_oob = "SOU_black_revolution_deserted_version"
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					SOV = {
						NOT = {
							has_country_flag = anarchist_hold_leningrad
						}
					}
				}
				load_oob = "SOU_naval_ships_black_revolution"
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_dlc = "Man the Guns"
					}
					SOV = {
						NOT = {
							has_country_flag = anarchist_hold_leningrad
						}
					}
				}
				load_oob = "SOU_naval_ships_black_revolution_nomtg"
			}
		}
	}
}

#The Trials Begin

	title = soviets.409.t
	desc = soviets.409.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_detained_china

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = soviets.410 days = 30 }
		}
	}

	option = { #Very well
		name = soviets.409.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		set_country_flag = sov_trials_begin
		set_variable = { time_remaining_before_end_trials = 200 }
	}
}

#End of the Black Revolution - Civil War
country_event = {
	id = soviets.412
	title = soviets.412.t
	desc = soviets.412.d
	picture = GFX_soldiers_with_guns_russia2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = soviets.412.a
		set_country_flag = end_of_the_revolution
		clr_country_flag = black_revolution_civil_war_in_progress
		add_ideas = SOV_no_export_anarchy
		custom_effect_tooltip = end_revolution_focus_available
		custom_effect_tooltip = division_will_be_locked_anarchy
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = SOU
				}
				remove_core_of = SOU
			}
		}
		add_threat = -5
		remove_ideas = SOV_Determination
		hidden_effect = {
			delete_unit_template_and_units = {
				division_template = "Militsiya Gornostrelkovaya Diviziya"
			}
			delete_unit_template_and_units = {
				division_template = "Povstancheskaya Militsiya Diviziya"
			}
			delete_unit_template_and_units = {
				division_template = "Militsiya Motorizirovannaya Diviziya"
			}
			delete_unit_template_and_units = {
				division_template = "Militsiya Kavaleriyskaya Diviziya"
			}
			set_division_template_lock = {
				division_template = "Povstancheskaya Diviziya"
				is_locked = yes
			}
			set_division_template_lock = {
				division_template = "Gornostrelkovaya Diviziya"
				is_locked = yes
			}
			set_division_template_lock = {
				division_template = "Motorizirovannaya Povstancheskaya Diviziya"
				is_locked = yes
			}
			set_division_template_lock = {
				division_template = "Kavaleriyskaya Povstancheskaya Diviziya"
				is_locked = yes
			}
			set_division_template_lock = {
				division_template = "Tankovaya Povstancheskaya Diviziya"
				is_locked = yes
			}
			set_division_template_lock = {
				division_template = "Vozdushno-Desantnaya Brigada"
				is_locked = yes
			}
			set_division_template_lock = {
				division_template = "Strelkovaya Diviziya"
				is_locked = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = SOV_Surprise_attack_black_revolution
			}
			remove_ideas = SOV_Surprise_attack_black_revolution
		}
	}
}

#Hidden Event to create state flag for Send Recon Units without making a mess
country_event = {
	id = soviets.414

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	hidden = yes

	immediate = {
		set_variable = { sov_count_state_recon = 0 }
		while_loop_effect = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = sov_count_state_recon
					value = 80
					compare = less_than
				}
			}
			
			random_scope_in_array = {
				array = SOV.owned_controlled_states
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_state_flag = recon_units_scout_place
						has_state_flag = small_counter_revolution_resistance_1
						has_state_flag = small_counter_revolution_resistance_2
						has_state_flag = small_counter_revolution_resistance_3
						has_state_flag = medium_counter_revolution_resistance_1
						has_state_flag = medium_counter_revolution_resistance_2
						has_state_flag = large_counter_revolution_resistance_1
						state = 219
						state = 137
						state = 195
						state = 217
						state = 408
						state = 202
					}
				}
				
				remove_from_array = { SOV.sov_recon_rebel_anarchy_states = THIS }
				THIS = {
					set_state_flag = recon_units_scout_place
				}
			}

			add_to_variable = { sov_count_state_recon = 1 }
		}
	}
}

		hidden_effect = {

		add_political_power = 100

		add_to_variable = { united_russia_strength = 2 }

			add_idea = SOV_Black_guard_army_3
		}

		remove_ideas = SOV_Black_guard_army_2
		add_ideas = SOV_Black_guard_reformation

	desc = soviets.451.d
	picture = GFX_handshake_russia2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Welcome Home Brothers
		name = soviets.451.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = UKR
				is_owned_and_controlled_by = UKR
			}
			SOV = {
				add_state_core = PREV
			}
		}
		SOV = {
			annex_country = {
				target = UKR
				transfer_troops = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

#Russia Biggest threat
country_event = {
	id = soviets.486
	title = soviets.486.t
	desc = soviets.486.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_military_parade

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #The Allies
		name = soviets.486.a
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 33
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_opinion = {
						target = ENG
						value > 50
					}
					has_opinion = {
						target = FRA
						value > 50
					}
				}
			}
		}
		ENG = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = SOV
				modifier = russian_hostility
			}
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = alliance
				id = SOV
				value = -25
			}
		}
		FRA = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = SOV
				modifier = russian_hostility
			}
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = alliance
				id = SOV
				value = -25
			}
		}
		add_ideas = SOV_Allies_menace
	}

	option = { #The Fascist

		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 33
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_opinion = {
						target = GER
						value > 50

					has_opinion = {
						target = ITA
						value > 50
					}
				}
			}
		}
		GER = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = SOV
				modifier = russian_hostility
			}
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = alliance
				id = SOV
				value = -25
			}
		}
		ITA = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = SOV
				modifier = russian_hostility
			}
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = alliance
				id = SOV
				value = -25
			}
		}

			factor = 33
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_opinion = {
					target = JAP

			factor = 33
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = unlock_vladimir_as_politician
		set_country_flag = vladimir_politician_advisor_chosen
	}

	option = { #He shall Lead an Army
		name = soviets.487.b
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 33
		}
		create_field_marshal = {
			name = "Vladimir Kirillovich"
			picture = "Portrait_Vladimir_Kirillovich.dds"
			traits = { politically_connected media_personality }
			skill = 3
			attack_skill = 2
			defense_skill = 3
			planning_skill = 2
			logistics_skill = 2
		}
	}

	option = { #He shall be a military advisor
		name = soviets.487.c
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 33
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = unlock_vladimir_as_chief_advisor
		set_country_flag = vladimir_military_advisor_chosen
		show_ideas_tooltip = SOV_vladimir_kirillovich_military_advisor
	}
}

					has_dlc = "Man the Guns"
				}
			}

			}
		}
	}

			limit = {

					has_country_flag = has_trained_mountaineers_for_civil_war

						has_country_flag = control_caucasus
					}
				}
			}
			SOV = {
				load_oob = "SOV_elite_mountaineers_no_caucasus_civil_war"
			}
		}

					has_country_flag = control_caucasus
				}
			}
			SOV = {
				load_oob = "SOV_elite_mountaineers_has_caucasus_civil_war"
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				SOV = {
					has_country_flag = has_engaged_italian_division_for_civil_war
				}
			}
			SOV = {
				load_oob = "SOV_italian_volunteers_caucasus_civil_war"
			}
		}
	}
}

	hidden = yes

	trigger = {
		country_exists = SOV
		SOV = {
			has_idea = SOV_Unified_komintern_red_armies
			is_faction_leader = yes
		}
		NOT = {
			original_tag = SOV
			has_idea = SOV_Unified_komintern_red_armies
		}
		is_in_faction_with = SOV
		has_war_together_with = SOV
		has_government = communism
	}

	immediate = {
		add_ideas = SOV_Unified_komintern_red_armies
	}
}
